***depressie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:depressie.html>depressie</a> (7654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">dépression</i> and/or directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">depressio</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:depressie.html>depressie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:depressies.html>depressies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:depressie.html>depressietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A physical depression</li>
<li>A psychologically 'low' state of mind, producing serious long-term lowering of enjoyment</li>
<li>A low physical pressure</li>
<li>A meteorological depression, (area of) low air pressure</li>
<li>A long low in the economic situation</li>
<li>A downward pressure, position or movement</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inzinking.html>inzinking</a></span></li>
<li>(psychological) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:depressiviteit.html>depressiviteit</a></span></li></ul>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:depressie.html>depressie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>

<p>Unstressed form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">there</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_3">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>there</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Article">Article</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive singular feminine of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i></span></span>; of the.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geschiedenis.html>geschiedenis</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a></b> Nederlandsche <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">history of the Dutch language</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i></span></span>; of the.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koninkrijk.html>koninkrijk</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a></b> Nederlanden</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the kingdom of the Netherlands</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">dative singular feminine of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i></span></span>.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>Only the nominative forms are common in modern usage. Accusative and dative forms are archaic and limited to fixed expressions. Genitive forms, while still productive and regiolectal, are not part of the standardized varieties and mainly reserved for poetic and literary language. They are also found as part of surnames.</li>
<li>* The current pronunciation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a spelling pronunciation. Before the word became archaic, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> pronounced with a schwa, <span class="IPA">/dər/</span>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:derden.html>derden</a> (40913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:derrie.html>derrie</a> (107715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dari</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">darrie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">darinc</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">darink</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:derrie.html>derrie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now chiefly specialist<span class="ib-comma">,</span> geology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> geography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> peat contaminated with <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></li>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:geologie.html>geologie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diepe.html>diepe</a>, donkerkleurige veenlaag</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dertene</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dertiene</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thritēn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thritien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þritehun</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">trettjin</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">dreizehn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thirteen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">tretten</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dertig.html>dertig</a> (1911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dertich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thrītig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þrīz tigiwiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_2">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>thirty</li></ol>

***des.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> (2540)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Article">Article</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive singular <span class="inflection-of-conjoined">masculine<span class="inflection-of-sep">/</span>neuter</span> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Note that normally only the nominative <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used. The other forms are archaic, but survive in numerous idiomatic expressions such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huizes.html>huizes</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:morgens.html>morgens</a></i> (itself archaic and shortened, like similar expressions, to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">'s <a href = vnd.unilang:morgens.html>morgens</a></i> in contemporary Dutch).</li>
<li>The current pronunciation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a spelling pronunciation. Before the word became archaic, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> pronounced with a schwa, <span class="IPA">/dəs/</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">'s</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_2">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>the ... the (<i>used as an intensifier to indicate the degree of an action</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>Des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaker.html>vaker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rug.html>rug</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toekeren.html>toekeren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beter.html>beter</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The more often people turn their back at <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> the better!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Lidwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:lidwoord.html>Lidwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a></b>
</p>

***desinformatie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:desinformatie.html>desinformatie</a> (84038)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in the 1950s, becoming common in the late 1970s. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дезинформа́ция</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dezinformácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">désinformation</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">des-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:informatie.html>informatie</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:desinformatie.html>desinformatie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">disinformation</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">dissemination of intentionally false information</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>1954</b> July 1, "Gevluchte ambassade-secretaris Petrof: Sovjet-spionnage in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zes.html>zes</a> MVD-afdelingen", <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Volkskrant</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 32, No. 9006, page 3.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dessert.html>dessert</a> (7449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:dessert.html>dessert</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">desservir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">disserve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">dés-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dis-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">servir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">serve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, thus literally meaning “removal of what <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> served”.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>then (at that time)
<dl><dd><i>Vollenhove <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> in 936 <a href = vnd.unilang:vermeld.html>vermeld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> 'Fulnaho'. <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebied.html>gebied</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:destijds.html>destijds</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woud.html>woud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigendom.html>eigendom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:otto.html>Otto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>Grote</a>.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/VollenhoveGeschiedenis">[1]</a></sup>  |  Vollenhove <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> already in 936 mentioned as 'Fulnaho'. The region <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> at that time a forest that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the property of <a href = vnd.unilang:otto.html>Otto</a> the Great.</dd></dl></li></ol>

***deuce.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deuce.html>deuce</a> (17222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">dewes</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">two</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">duo</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:deuce.html>deuce</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:deuces.html>deuces</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A card with two <a href = vnd.unilang:pips.html>pips</a>, one of four in a standard deck of playing cards.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dice games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A side of a <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> with two <a href = vnd.unilang:spots.html>spots</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dice games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cast of dice totalling two.</li>
<li>The number two.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">tennis</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tied game where either player can win by scoring two consecutive points.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">baseball</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A curveball.</li>
<li>A '32 <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ford" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ford">Ford</a>.
<ul><li><b>1978</b>, Mayall, <a href = vnd.unilang:joe.html>Joe</a>. "Driving Impression: Reproduction <b><a href = vnd.unilang:deuce.html>Deuce</a></b> Hiboy", in <i>Rod Action</i>, p.26</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> 2-barrel (twin choke) carburetors <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in the phrase <i>3 <a href = vnd.unilang:deuces.html>deuces</a></i>: an arrangement on a common intake manifold</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:restaurants.html>restaurants</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A table seating two <a href = vnd.unilang:diners.html>diners</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Canada, US<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of excrement.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">piece of <a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <i>See</i> Thesaurus:defecation</li></ul>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dusius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">phantom, specter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scottish_Gaelic" class="extiw" title="w:Scottish Gaelic">Scottish Gaelic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gd">taibhs</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gd">taibhse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">apparition, ghost</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a></i> (compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deity</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">epithet</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The Devil, <span class="use-with-mention">used in exclamations of confusion or anger.</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deugniet.html>deugniet</a> (20355)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deugen.html>deugen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be good</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; parallel to cognate <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Taugenichts</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">døgenigt</i> (the latter of which <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> on a somewhat different sense).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>(originally) good-for-nothing</li>
<li>(usually) <a href = vnd.unilang:rascal.html>rascal</a>, scamp, a naughty boy</li>
<li>(term of <a href = vnd.unilang:endearment.html>endearment</a>) knave, amusing boy</li></ol>

***deus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a> (76453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Galician-Portuguese" class="extiw" title="w:Galician-Portuguese">Old Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="roa-opt"><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a>, deity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, unusual in that it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> derived from the nominative instead of the accusative (<i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:deum.html>deum</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Old Latin">Old Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="itc-ola">deivos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a>, deity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro">*deiwos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a>, deity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*deywós</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a>, deity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dyew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sky, heaven</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="pt"><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-pt p-form-of" lang="pt">deuses</b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-pt f-form-of" lang="pt">deusa</b>, <i>feminine plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-pt f | p-form-of" lang="pt">deusas</b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-pt f-form-of" lang="pt">deia</b> <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">poetic</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>, <i>feminine plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-pt f | p-form-of" lang="pt">deias</b>)

***deuterium.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deuterium.html>deuterium</a> (35226)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***devies.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:devies.html>devies</a> (40909)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">devise</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">devise</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">devise</i>. The financial senses <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Devise</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">devise</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:devies.html>devies</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deviezen.html>deviezen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:motto.html>motto</a>, slogan, watchword</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> security (proof for ownership of <a href = vnd.unilang:bonds.html>bonds</a>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance<span class="ib-comma">,</span> economy<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <span class="deprecated-label">plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> money or an asset in a foreign currency</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>this (masculine, feminine); <span class="use-with-mention">referring to a thing or a person <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a> by.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this tree</span></div></dd>
